TITLE      The phenomenological optical potential for             D025700100003 
           alpha-scattering from nuclei in the Ca region          D025700100004 
AUTHOR     (H.P.Gubler,U.Kiebele,H.O.Meyer,G.R.Plattner,I.Sick)   D025700100005 
INSTITUTE  (2SWTBAS)                                              D025700100006 
REFERENCE  (J,NP/A,351,29,1981)                                   D025700100007

FACILITY   (CYCLO) The injector cyclotron facility                D025700100009 
METHOD     (EDE)                                                  D025700100010 
SAMPLE     The Ca targets were fabricated by evaporating natural  D025700100011 
           Ca (with a 40Ca content of 96.6%) onto self-supporting D025700100012 
           carbon foils of 20 mu-g/cm2 thickness. Target          D025700100013 
           densities of 200-400 mu-g/cm2 were used.               D025700100014 
           The 50Ti and the 52Cr targets consisted of             D025700100015 
           self-supporting foils. These isotopically enriched     D025700100016 
           targets contained 83.2% 50Ti, 12.4% 48Ti and 99.9% 52CrD025700100017 
DETECTOR   (SIBAR) Three surface barrier detectors with a         D025700100018 
           sensitive thickness of 1 mm served to measure the      D025700100019 
           forward-angle data.                                    D025700100020 
           (PSSSD) Two position-sensitive detectors, each         D025700100021 
           covering an angular range of 12degr., were used at     D025700100022 
           backward angles.                                       D025700100023 
           Three fixed detectors, at 161. degr. and at +-15degr., D025700100024 
           served as monitors of the target, beam intensity and   D025700100025 
           incident beam direction.                               D025700100026 
           (TELES) The measurements at the energies higher than   D025700100027 
           50 MeV were made with telescopes of 2 or 3 fully       D025700100028 
           depleted detectors of 1 mm sensitive thickness stacked D025700100029 
           in series to allow for the greater range of scattered  D025700100030 
           alpha -particles.                                      D025700100031 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR1) Uncertainty in the absolute normalization. D025700100032 
           The target thickness was determined by energy-loss     D025700100033 
           measurements of 5.9 MeV alpha-particles. The estimated D025700100034 
           accurancy is 20%. To obtain a consistent normalization D025700100035 
           of cross section data, the measurements were made for  D025700100036 
           the different targets overlapping in energy and angle. D025700100037 
           (DATA-ERR2) Uncertainty from statistics and            D025700100038 
           angle accurancy                                        D025700100039

            who received them from authors                        D025700100041
